[11-Nov-21 10:56 AM] ApexChat#8127

[11-Nov-21 10:58 AM] ApexChat#8127

[11-Nov-21 10:59 AM] ApexChat#8127

[26-Apr-22 11:24 AM] ApexChat#8127
**cellozzo**:	ok, interesting, so based on the structure and lvl built on the planet the MANAGER has to pay for upkeep, and the infrastructure gave a bonus or some such thing?


[26-Apr-22 11:25 AM] ApexChat#8127
**TheDoctor1786**:	Kinda! So there are two different types of upkeep


[26-Apr-22 11:25 AM] ApexChat#8127
**TheDoctor1786**:	There's COGC upkeep which funds the program that provides planetwide bonuses (25% construction bonus for Danakil)


[26-Apr-22 11:26 AM] ApexChat#8127
**TheDoctor1786**:	And then there's Population Infrastructure upkeep which funds the buildings that keep workers happy and continuing to migrate to / not leave your planet


[26-Apr-22 11:27 AM] ApexChat#8127
**TheDoctor1786**:	So the population infrastructure doesn't really get a bonus, but it promotes worker stability and growth


[26-Apr-22 11:29 AM] ApexChat#8127
**TheDoctor1786**:	This has a LOT of detail but goes beyond the wiki in its explanation of planetary populations


[26-Apr-22 11:29 AM] ApexChat#8127
**TheDoctor1786**:	https://pct.fnar.net/population-infrastructure/

**Jets0n**:	Consumable supplies at Base - Moon are running low.


[21-Aug-23 02:30 AM] ApexChat#8127
**Jets0n**:	what are those supplies?


[21-Aug-23 03:54 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	worker consumables, RAT, DW, OVE, COF, PWO, note, it won't complain about luxury ones if you never supplied them, but it will do so when you start to run low


[21-Aug-23 04:01 AM] ApexChat#8127
**Jets0n**:	Thanks


[21-Aug-23 04:06 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	it sends out a warning when you have less than 3 days worth at current consumption, note that if it consumes less than 1 unit per day it'll flag it at 3 left (even if you only consume 0.1 per day (happens on higher tier workers fairly often, mostly since you usually don't have a lot of them in a base))


[21-Aug-23 04:07 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	I should also add, it works for all worker tiers, I only listed the pioneer tier stuff since your new, but realized that could be misleading for you later on, but those are the only ones you need to worry about for now


[21-Aug-23 04:08 AM] ApexChat#8127
**Jets0n**:	is PPA considered as a consumable as well or i should better buy RATs instead of producing PPA?


[21-Aug-23 04:08 AM] ApexChat#8127
**Jets0n**:	do they consume H2o or it must be DW?


[21-Aug-23 04:19 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	PPA is not a consumable, you can open you base screen, and click the workforce tab to see what your daily demand is for each item


[21-Aug-23 04:19 AM] ApexChat#8127
**DogeConomy**:	PPA is very unprofitable in the long run


[21-Aug-23 04:20 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	DW is drinking water, it's made from H2O though, but they are separate items and H2O can't be used in it's place, think of H2O as straight out of the ground from an unclean water source, while DW has been through a purification plant to bring it up to standand


[21-Aug-23 04:21 AM] ApexChat#8127
**DogeConomy**:	There's little demand for PPA, and one/ two food processors in the whole of the Moria region could satisfy the market demand


[21-Aug-23 04:22 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	each higher tier of worker requires more and more difficult to make consumables, and luzury consumables often require some input from a higher tier worker to make (exception, scientists, the highest tier of worker)


[21-Aug-23 04:22 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	also that, PPA is a bit of a newbie trap unfortunately, due to how the list is ordered


[21-Aug-23 04:24 AM] ApexChat#8127

[10-Jan-24 04:15 AM] ApexChat#8127
***Deepimpact** joined.*


[10-Jan-24 05:14 AM] ApexChat#8127
**YourFavoriteMike**:	Can I ask what a POPR run is?


[10-Jan-24 05:16 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	population report, it's a 1 week time peroid, I forget when, but it's either monday to monday, or sunday to sunday


[10-Jan-24 05:51 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	during the report, work forces are rebalanced, as each planet only has so many workers, most of the time, especially early on, this won't matter, as all starter planets, and most common expansion, have enough workers, at least at the lower tier of worker, that you won't hit the limit


[10-Jan-24 05:51 AM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	*more advance player lesson coming up* to maintain planet populations, governors are elected, and it's what the tax on production runs goes towards paying for (as such, existing governors get one hell of an advantage over new runners, as a bad governor can shut a planet down for a month), either through buying or paying for the production of population infrastructure items and upgrading the infrastructure in general, as well as paying for CoCG (chamber of global commerce) upkeep


[10-Jan-24 05:51 AM] ApexChat#8127
**YourFavoriteMike**:	That's pretty intricate.  Thank you for the explanation


[10-Jan-24 05:51 AM] ApexChat#8127
**YourFavoriteMike**:	So as a new player, doesn't really affect me too much it sounds like


[10-Jan-24 11:39 AM] ApexChat#8127
**S3KT355**:	@yourfavoritemike while the POPI upkeep and the specifics of governing don't affect you per say, you do still get the ability to vote for who is governor. if you're looking at the PLI for danakil (which should be a part of your starter HQ screen), you'll see a hyperlink under infrastructure called the planetary administration center. if you click that, you'll see the upcoming term and next to the candidates are two greyed out vote buttons. when the election starts, you'll get one vote that you can commit to whichever candidate you want. even if you don't understand much about the governor's race or keeping up with a planet, i highly encourage you to still at least get involved in the voting process and voice any opinions you may have about how the planet is being run or what you think should change, because otherwise we won't know how to fix the problems you're having :D


[10-Jan-24 01:25 PM] ApexChat#8127
***Nanolink08** left.*


[10-Jan-24 03:40 PM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	why I flagged it as a more advance player lesson, there is a lot that goes into running a planet, from goverment programs, taxes on each type of building, population infrastructure (and figuring out the most cost effective way to maintain required population for each workforce tier). most existing major planets have figured out the answer to these questions, but it's also why when 2 people run for governor, the existing one will win 90% of the time, as I said above, a bad governor can shut a planet down for a month (via maxing out taxes to insane levels, and not maintaining any of the population infrastructure). That being said, sometimes a governor retires, ie, doesn't run again and we have to choose a new one, or has something happen that means he can't do his job properly and majorly effects the planets usefulness, in which case a new governor can take over for someone not doing their job properly


[10-Jan-24 03:40 PM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	all starter planets have a healthy excess of low tier populations, as well as most common expansions from said starter planets (I won't say all because there might be 1 that is the exception), more advance planets might still have problems with that, but planets that favor high tier populations for whatever reasons will still have this problem (this is more mid to late game though). The reason is that high tier populations are rather expensive to maintain for a governor, so they try and run as little excess as possible


[10-Jan-24 03:40 PM] ApexChat#8127
**bazdakka**:	basically, you won't need this knowledge for at least a couple of months, but it's worth paying attention to when discussions about it happen in chat, this planet is actually a really good one for it due to the current higher tier population shortages on this planet, so there will be discussions about it in this chat

**bazdakka**:	hmm, looks like some upgrades might be needed, those are expensive, though short term supplying more materials will do, I'd suggest something that does safety, since higher tier concerns are capped by lower tier ones (tier one is life support, tier 2 is safety and health, tier 3 is comfort and culture, tier 4 is education), ie, the highest a tier can go is the lower of the ones for the previous tier, in out case, comfort and culture can't be raised higher than our safety (current lowest of safety and health), so to raise them, we need to raise safety first, and health not long after, both the easy buildings have been upgraded to level 10 already (rather expensive, but this is the right planet for it), but it may be worth looking at getting other buildings, or just accepting that we need to supply 2 upkeep materials permanently from now on

[21-May-24 12:43 PM] ApexChat#8127
**TeurasSika**:	so wait even when we have tech unemployment 0%, if I were to build PP3 now technicians would come to fill it at next POPR?


[21-May-24 12:49 PM] ApexChat#8127
**Snowfzy**:	Not necessarily, especially since there's 93 open jobs, jobs that haven't been filled with technicians


[21-May-24 12:50 PM] ApexChat#8127
**Snowfzy**:	Dunno the exact mechanic for this kind of situation


[21-May-24 01:06 PM] ApexChat#8127
**Ogrebeef-Backkicker**:	The [open jobs] number refers to jobs waiting to be filled before the last POPR ran.  The [change] number shows the number of workers that were added on that last POPR.    Since there were 93 open jobs and a change of 152 all those jobs were filled and there were 59 unemployed workers afterwards.  The unemployed workers go into the planetary pool and each base can take up to 10% from that pool during the week.  When the next POPR runs any remaining unemployed workers will be distributed.


[21-May-24 01:10 PM] ApexChat#8127
**Ogrebeef-Backkicker**:	So if you now build a PP3 which requires 40 technicians you will get 6 (rounded up from 5.9) workers... assuming 10 other people haven't already built stuff that used up all 59 unemployed workers.  When the next POPR runs if there are enough available workers then you will get the remaining 34 that you need.


[21-May-24 02:13 PM] ApexChat#8127
**TeurasSika**:	I see, thanks for spelling the mechanic out for me! So to cut to the chase, I'm guessing if I were to construct PP3(s) I could maybe expect to fill them with technicians in a couple of weeks (with the current status of Danakil)? :D

If your HABS will only support 950 workers then it may be a waste to build that final production building.
